REGULAR MEETING MINUTES 
 
March 22, 2024 
9:15 AM

remote meeting by interactive conference technology, via Microsoft Teams, 
http://tinyurl.com/2p9zhjr2.

Floor, 200 S. High Street, Wailuku, Hawaii. 
 
Video recording of meeting available at: www.mauicounty.legistar.com

CR 24-33 Recommending FILING of Bill 40 (2024) to amend the Fiscal Year 2024 
Budget, by: 1) amending Section 2, Estimated Revenues, by increasing 
Carryover/Savings from the General Fund by $7,304,000 and Interfund 
Transfers by $7,304,000; 2) amending Section 3.B.4 .g.(6), Department of 
Finance, Countywide Costs, Supplemental Transfer to the Solid Waste Fund, by 
increasing Category B (Operations and Equipment) and Total appropriations by 
$7,304,000; 3) amending Section 4.A.1.a.(1), Department of Environmental 
Management, Countywide, Sanitation, by adding a new appropriation for Solid 
Waste Management Fund, entitled “Lāhainā Wildfire Disposal Sites,” in the 
amount of $7,304,000; 4) adjusting the totals accordingly; and 5) amending 
Appendix C - Capital Improvement Proje cts, Department of Environmental 
Management, Countywide, by adding a new project and project description, 
entitled “Lāhainā Wildfire Disposal Sites,” in the amount of $7,304,000.  
 
CR 24-34 Recommending FIRST READING of Bill 33 (2024) to amend the Fiscal 
Year 2024 Budget by amending Section 3.B.1., Department of Agriculture, by: 1) 
deleting “the” from the Department title; 2) reducing the appropriation for 
Agriculture Program, Category B (Operations and Equipment) by $28,239; 3) 
reducing the appropriation f or Grants and disbursements for Agricultural 
Promotion, Feral Animal Recovery by $781,500; 4) reducing the appropriation 
for Grants and disbursements for Agricultural Promotion, Agriculture Education 
and Apprenticeship by $51,600; 5) increasing the appropr iation for Grants and 
disbursements for Agricultural Promotion, Agriculture Promotion/Technology by 
$861,339; 6) reducing the conditional amount under Grants and disbursements 
for Agricultural Promotion, Agriculture Promotion/Technology for 
“infrastructure improvements on established agricultural operations” by 
$45,000; and 7) adjusting the totals accordingly. 
 
CR 24-35 Recommending FIRST READING of Bill 37 (2024) to amend the Fiscal 
Year 2024 Budget, Appendix C - Capital Improvement Projects, Department of 
Fire and Public Safety, Wailuku-Kahului Community Plan Area, by revising the 
project description for the Administration Building Acquisition by deleting “Site 
selection and land acquisition to construct” and inserting in its place “Planning  
and conceptual drawings for.”  
 7 
 
CR 24-36 Recommending FIRST READING of Bill 7 (2024) to amend Chapter 
3.47, Maui County Code, to require the Director of Finance to submit quarterly 
reports to the Council that include: 1) the number of County transient 
accommodations and estimated taxes grouped by residency area where the 
transient accommodation is located; 2) the number of County transient 
accommodations grouped by the taxpayer’s mailing address; and 3) an aged 
accounts receivable list of delinquent County transient accommodations; and to 
prevent the destruction of monthly, quarterly, or semiannual returns filed under 
Section 3.47.070, Maui County Code, in certain situations.

PROVIDED THAT THE REMAINDER OF THE LOT IS USED FOR PREDOMINANT ACTIVE OF
